empowering project and service managers in managing the associated risks and resourc-

--- Document Chunk 4943 ---
es without prejudice to the Ao/Aod powers.

--- Document Chunk 4944 ---
The iAs is the internal auditor of the Agency and performs independent assessment on 

--- Document Chunk 4945 ---
the internal control systems based on a three-year plan. Complementary, internal audits 

--- Document Chunk 4946 ---
are performed. The external audit is performed by the European Court of Auditors (for the 

--- Document Chunk 4947 ---
legality and regularity of transactions) and an external company (for the accounts).

--- Document Chunk 4948 ---
Internal controls tools include:

--- Document Chunk 4949 ---
  Controls performed at all levels of the Agency 

--- Document Chunk 4950 ---
  Risk management, in particular at project/service level and Agency level where 

--- Document Chunk 4951 ---
the most significant/relevant risks are captured including strategic risks (recorded 

--- Document Chunk 4952 ---
in the agency/corporate risk register and reported in the CAAR). Risks are formally 

--- Document Chunk 4953 ---
assessed at both inherent and residual level to make sure that the analysis of the 

--- Document Chunk 4954 ---
effectiveness of the controls in place is ensured before additional mitigating meas-

--- Document Chunk 4955 ---
ures are put in place (cost-effectiveness of controls). 

--- Document Chunk 4956 ---
  Corrective/preventive measures are established when recurrent and systemic er -

--- Document Chunk 4957 ---
rors are recorded. Ex-ante nonconformities involving significant amount of money 

--- Document Chunk 4958 ---
(>15.000 euros) are approved by the Ao

--- Document Chunk 4959 ---
  internal control monitoring criteria for measuring the presence and the function -

--- Document Chunk 4960 ---
ing of the principles are in process of being developed considering the risk envi -

--- Document Chunk 4961 ---
ronment and are focused more on effectiveness and efficiency.

--- Document Chunk 4962 ---
  Follow-up of recommendations from ECA, iAs, discharge authority as well as other 

--- Document Chunk 4963 ---
sources (e.g. external evaluations) to ensure that the actions plans are effectively 

--- Document Chunk 4964 ---
implemented within the agreed deadlines.

--- Document Chunk 4965 ---
  An integrated reporting system to inform and alert management on the progress 

--- Document Chunk 4966 ---
on the implementation of costs for each project/service as well as sPd outputs 

--- Document Chunk 4967 ---
(monthly dashboard). The cost data is connected to the source (suMMA). i t in -

--- Document Chunk 4968 ---
cludes several other parameters such as risks, issues, changes, corrective actions 

--- Document Chunk 4969 ---
taken, quality, milestones etc.

--- Document Chunk 4970 ---
  Budgetary status reports are produced on a daily basis including an overview 

--- Document Chunk 4971 ---
per unit of the budget execution per budget line for all fund sources, financial 

--- Document Chunk 4972 ---
information on commitments, payments and transfers, information on progress of 

--- Document Chunk 4973 ---
planned procurement and contracts. The information helps achieving the perfor -

--- Document Chunk 4974 ---
mance targets in these particular areas.

--- Document Chunk 4975 ---
  Ex-ante controls consisting in several checks of financial and operational aspects 

--- Document Chunk 4976 ---
of transactions by the actors involved in the financial circuits. There is a very com -

--- Document Chunk 4977 ---
prehensive checklist/templates as well as guidance which ensure an effective level 

--- Document Chunk 4978 ---
of control. The specific controls are detailed in the manual of financial procedures 

--- Document Chunk 4979 ---
which also included the steps to be taken for making a financial transaction, the 

--- Document Chunk 4980 ---
various financial circuits by type of transaction and the different roles and responsi-

--- Document Chunk 4981 ---
bilities. The Agency is putting substantial efforts in updated these manuals/check-

--- Document Chunk 4982 ---
lists.

--- Document Chunk 4983 ---
  Ex-post controls for payments not subject to an ex-ante verification. The material-

--- Document Chunk 4984 ---
ity criterion defined by the A o/Aods for drawing a reservation in the CAAR is an 

--- Document Chunk 4985 ---
assessment of whether more than 2% of the payments of the activity concerned 

--- Document Chunk 4986 ---
is erroneous. 

--- Document Chunk 4987 ---
  sensitive function policy defines the management of functions involving a consid-

--- Document Chunk 4988 ---
erable amount of autonomy and executive powers with the aim of ensuring that 

--- Document Chunk 4989 ---
actions are taken to mitigate the risk that the jobholders deliberately misuse their 

--- Document Chunk 4990 ---
decision-making powers or influence with a view to gaining personal advantages 

--- Document Chunk 4991 ---
sTRATEgy FoR  ThE oRgAnisATionAL  MAnAgEMEnT  And inTERnAL  ConTRoL sysTEMs  | 111

--- Document Chunk 4992 ---
  Ad-hoc controls are additionally applied at the level of processes whenever the 

--- Document Chunk 4993 ---
management assesses it is necessary to mitigate a specific risk (e.g. selection pro -

--- Document Chunk 4994 ---
cedures, financial delegations).

--- Document Chunk 4995 ---
The Agency’s anti-fraud strategy has been developed in accordance with oLAF guidelines, 

--- Document Chunk 4996 ---
it is setting clear objectives, actions and responsibilities and it is based on a standalone 

--- Document Chunk 4997 ---
fraud risk assessment exercise adapted to the Agency’s environment encompassing fraud 

--- Document Chunk 4998 ---
risks regardless of their criticality. The risk of fraud is duly considered when carry out the 

--- Document Chunk 4999 ---
risk assessment exercise. 

--- Document Chunk 5000 ---
The strategy is focusing on three objectives:

--- Document Chunk 5001 ---
  handle effectively actual or perceived conflict of interest,

--- Document Chunk 5002 ---
  Enhance the promotion of high ethical values as well as increasing fraud aware -

--- Document Chunk 5003 ---
ness

--- Document Chunk 5004 ---
  Enhance data and information security

--- Document Chunk 5005 ---
The objectives are fully aligned with the fraud risks identified which include inherent sig -

--- Document Chunk 5006 ---
nificant risk of conflict of interest due to specific circumstances of the Agency’s activities 

--- Document Chunk 5007 ---
(i.e. regulatory powers with significant decision making powers and potential reputational, 

--- Document Chunk 5008 ---
legal and financial consequences if conflict of interest not adequately managed; relatively 

--- Document Chunk 5009 ---
limited ‘market’ for recruitment of staff as well as for entities which could provide services 

--- Document Chunk 5010 ---
for the Agency), potential risk of cyber-attacks leading to operational damage, loss of data, 

--- Document Chunk 5011 ---
unauthorised disclosure of information or breach of data; potential risk of outsourcing the 

--- Document Chunk 5012 ---
data and information security without proper security risk assessment), risk of staff mem -

--- Document Chunk 5013 ---
bers not being fully aware of their ethics obligations as well as handling and reporting 

--- Document Chunk 5014 ---
fraud. The Agency has put in place comprehensive control measures proportional to the 

--- Document Chunk 5015 ---
level of risks and amount of risk identified which encompass (but not limited to) manda -

--- Document Chunk 5016 ---
tory tailor-made trainings on ethics and separately on antifraud for all staff, mandatory 

--- Document Chunk 5017 ---
submission of declaration of interests for all staff and members of the Management Board 

--- Document Chunk 5018 ---
and of the Board of Appeal, ex-post/on the spot controls, review of internal procedures 

--- Document Chunk 5019 ---
(including procedures for reporting and handling fraud). Control indicators enable assess-

--- Document Chunk 5020 ---
ment of effectiveness of the measures taken.

--- Document Chunk 5021 ---
Starting 2023, the Agency converges the following activities under a single service 

--- Document Chunk 5022 ---
(Internal Management and Control System – ERA.1158) to better support the assur-

--- Document Chunk 5023 ---
ance function:

--- Document Chunk 5024 ---
1. The internal management system coordination – the successor of the previous iMs 

--- Document Chunk 5025 ---
service, from which the iso certification component was dropped, while the focus 

--- Document Chunk 5026 ---
is placed on the iCF further implementation and monitoring;

--- Document Chunk 5027 ---
2. The internal control coordination;

--- Document Chunk 5028 ---
3. The central financial verification;

--- Document Chunk 5029 ---
4. The contact point for iAs, ECA and EP discharge follow-up.

--- Document Chunk 5030 ---
Assessment of the effectiveness of the management system

--- Document Chunk 5031 ---
The agency monitors continuously the efficiency and effectiveness of the internal Control 

--- Document Chunk 5032 ---
Framework. A yearly assessment report is produced where consideration is given to the 

--- Document Chunk 5033 ---
results of controls mentioned above. All the internal control components and principles 

--- Document Chunk 5034 ---
must be present and functioning well at all levels of the Agency to be considered effec -

--- Document Chunk 5035 ---
tive. The results of the assessment are reported in the CAAR.

--- Document Chunk 5190 ---
Annex XiV.  

--- Document Chunk 5191 ---
strengthening  

--- Document Chunk 5192 ---
Action Plan (sAP)  

--- Document Chunk 5193 ---
2023-2027

--- Document Chunk 5194 ---
1. Context

--- Document Chunk 5195 ---
in 2022, the Agency’s Management Board adopted the strengthening Plan prepared by 

--- Document Chunk 5196 ---
the Agency in close cooperation with the European Commission. The purpose of the 

--- Document Chunk 5197 ---
strengthening Plan is to make the strongest possible case in order to strengthen the 

--- Document Chunk 5198 ---
Agency with resources matching the level of ambition necessary for achieving the 

--- Document Chunk 5199 ---
important EC policy objectives for rail, in an effective and efficient manner, and 

--- Document Chunk 5200 ---
benefit from high levels of ambition and efficiency within ERA’s structure and 

--- Document Chunk 5201 ---
methods.

--- Document Chunk 5202 ---
with the document serving as a basis for the internal EC budget negotiations in 2022, the 

--- Document Chunk 5203 ---
Agency received a proposed increase of 12 TAs in 202292. while the additional TA allocation 

--- Document Chunk 5204 ---
is lower compared to the request from the strengthening Plan (12 TAs proposed out of the 

--- Document Chunk 5205 ---
22 TAs requested), it can offer a good basis for the Agency to proceed with the implemen-

--- Document Chunk 5206 ---
tation of the strengthening Plan. 

--- Document Chunk 5207 ---
A very important challenge is represented by the fact that the additional TA allocation 

--- Document Chunk 5208 ---
needs to be fully covered under the existing subsidy envelope. To make best use of this 

--- Document Chunk 5209 ---
TA allocation and considering the external constraints related to the indexation of salaries 

--- Document Chunk 5210 ---
and prices, the Agency is making a thorough assessment of its capacity to cover these 

--- Document Chunk 5211 ---
costs in a sustainable manner until the end of MFF 2021-2027. several measures are envis-

--- Document Chunk 5212 ---
aged, such as the time-phased hiring of the TAs. The budget constraint on the subsidy side 

--- Document Chunk 5213 ---
is therefore an element to be properly monitored and managed for the whole remaining 

--- Document Chunk 5214 ---
period of the current MFF. 

--- Document Chunk 5215 ---
The current document describes the plan of actions which the Agency will put in place in 

--- Document Chunk 5216 ---
the period 2023-2027 in order to implement the strengthening Plan, taking into consid -

--- Document Chunk 5217 ---
eration the level of additional staff allocation proposed by the EC. it is hereinafter referred 

--- Document Chunk 5218 ---
as sAP (strengthening Action Plan) 2023-2027. This builds on actions already taken up to 

--- Document Chunk 5219 ---
present to increase the efficiency of the support services and tools.

--- Document Chunk 5220 ---
2. What we want to achieve

--- Document Chunk 5221 ---
ERA has established an outcome-driven framework, placing strong emphasis on effec -

--- Document Chunk 5222 ---
tiveness (i.e. “doing the right things”), in line with the prioritisation of activities included in 

--- Document Chunk 5223 ---
the strengthening Plan. in parallel, a delivery structure based on Projects and services has 

--- Document Chunk 5224 ---
been established. outputs of projects and services are followed up and measured using a 

--- Document Chunk 5225 ---
dashboard approach.

--- Document Chunk 5226 ---
with the strengthening Plan, we will implement a series of improvement actions that 

--- Document Chunk 5227 ---
should enable to achieve the most appropriate outcomes with the resources available. 

--- Document Chunk 5228 ---
This is important not only to justify the additional resources requested by the Agency, but 

--- Document Chunk 5229 ---
also in order to demonstrate that European taxpayer’s money is used in the most effective 

--- Document Chunk 5230 ---

--- Document Chunk 5233 ---
way, so that the European railway system can develop towards attractiveness, efficiency, 

--- Document Chunk 5234 ---
and sustainability.

improvement actions will be assessed according to their impact as well as ease of imple -

--- Document Chunk 5236 ---
mentation. Quantitative targets are defined (mainly related to the respective FTEs) and fol-

lowed up/measured on a regular basis. The baseline is ERA sPd 2022 and the monitoring

3. Objectives, actions, indicators, and targets

--- Document Chunk 5241 ---
The sAP 2023-2027 mirrors the strengthening Plan and translated it into concrete actions. 

--- Document Chunk 5242 ---
it is based on the planning and monitoring framework and enablers already set up 

--- Document Chunk 5243 ---
by the Agency, which includes: 

--- Document Chunk 5244 ---
  the multi-annual planning in the sPd, with a clear focus on the intervention logic; 

--- Document Chunk 5245 ---
  the Agency’s performance dashboard, including reporting to the EB and the MB

--- Document Chunk 5246 ---
  the regular budget execution monitoring and reporting

--- Document Chunk 5247 ---
  the Consolidated Annual Activity Report.

--- Document Chunk 5248 ---
The annual work programmes will therefore be aligned to the priorities listed in the sAP , 

--- Document Chunk 5249 ---
which represents an anchor for the multi-annual planning in what the priority policy areas 

--- Document Chunk 5250 ---
are concerned. A direct tracking of sAP-related FTEs, outputs and targets will be includes 

--- Document Chunk 5251 ---
in the sPds.

--- Document Chunk 5252 ---
The sAP 2023-2027 is organised along the following components/objectives:

--- Document Chunk 5253 ---
a.)  drive an optimal resourcing of policy priority areas, matched by proportional out-

--- Document Chunk 5254 ---
puts and outcomes, including efficiency gains

--- Document Chunk 5255 ---
b.)  Maintain proper resourcing and further efficiency gains for the authority tasks

--- Document Chunk 5256 ---
c.)  Ensure a reduction in the Agency’s administrative FTE allocation while maintaining 

--- Document Chunk 5257 ---
regularity and legality

--- Document Chunk 5258 ---
d.)  Ensure the overall projected FTE evolution by 2027

--- Document Chunk 5259 ---
e.)  Ensure effective and efficient budget management (planning and execution), ap -

--- Document Chunk 5260 ---
propriate risk management

C. Ensure a reduction in the Agency’s administrative FTE allocation

--- Document Chunk 5778 ---
Note 1: This objective is referred to the administrative FTE allocation, but encompasses a wide scope (e.g. redeploying administrative posts to operational activities, redeploying technical staff who 

--- Document Chunk 5779 ---
currently cover administrative tasks to operational tasks activities).

--- Document Chunk 5780 ---
All references are to FTEs (not posts) to allow for counting savings and/or redeployments which account for partitions of one FTE.

--- Document Chunk 5781 ---
Note 2: The sequencing is thought as follows: 

--- Document Chunk 5782 ---
i.  Creating the capacity of potentially free FTEs through process leaning, including automation – as such, this does not account for a materialised saving, but is a pre-condition (step 

--- Document Chunk 5783 ---
C2)

--- Document Chunk 5784 ---
ii.  identifying the opportunities to materialise that capacity – this can happen at contract end points (step C3)

--- Document Chunk 5785 ---
iii.  having the FTEs freed from administrative work needs to be followed up by their actual redeployment in operational areas (step C4)

--- Document Chunk 5786 ---
102 		This	reflects	the	re-visited	assumptions	for	the	use	of	ERA	FTEs	for	VA,	SSC,	ERTMS	TA	compared	to	2022	and	also	embeds	a	component	of	efficiency	gains	through	simplification/automation	of	processes.

--- Document Chunk 5976 ---
Budget related

--- Document Chunk 5977 ---
Risk Risk 

--- Document Chunk 5978 ---
assessment Mitigating measures

--- Document Chunk 5979 ---
1. The Agency might not be in the position to hire all 12 TAs in 2023 due to subsidy 

--- Document Chunk 5980 ---
constraints. The inflation trend poses significant pressure on the Agency’s capacity to 

--- Document Chunk 5981 ---
cover the salary costs in the absence of sufficient additional Eu subsidy.

--- Document Chunk 5982 ---
4

--- Document Chunk 5983 ---
The Agency is carefully monitoring the budget execution to strike the optimal use of 

--- Document Chunk 5984 ---
the existing resources in the spirit of sound financial management, while flagging early 

--- Document Chunk 5985 ---
warning signals in case of subsidy gaps. we will react by an agile approach, having 

--- Document Chunk 5986 ---
reserve lists in place but only conclude employment contracts when the budgetary 

--- Document Chunk 5987 ---
means are available.

--- Document Chunk 5988 ---
2. The revenues from Fees and Charges are not under the full control of the Agency. 

--- Document Chunk 5989 ---
in particular, the volume of work can fluctuate due to seasonal trends during the year, 

--- Document Chunk 5990 ---
but also more structurally, upwards (e.g. the need for re-certification following dAC 

--- Document Chunk 5991 ---
deployment, go-everywhere trains etc.) or downwards (e.g. starting with the second 

--- Document Chunk 5992 ---
round of safety certification for the same Ru at ERA, the complexity of the issues and 

--- Document Chunk 5993 ---
checks might drop compared to the first round).

--- Document Chunk 5994 ---
4

--- Document Chunk 5995 ---
Human resources and internal communication related

--- Document Chunk 5996 ---
Risk Risk 

--- Document Chunk 5997 ---
assessment Mitigating measures

--- Document Chunk 5998 ---
3. The changes in the working patterns, together with the financial consideration for 

--- Document Chunk 5999 ---
hiring at lower grades, might limit the attractiveness for the specialised technical jobs 

--- Document Chunk 6000 ---
offered by the Agency in the future. This might hamper the business continuity, talent 

--- Document Chunk 6001 ---
pool retention and by consequence, Agency’s capacity to deliver the technical outputs 

--- Document Chunk 6002 ---
envisaged in this plan.

--- Document Chunk 6003 ---
3

--- Document Chunk 6004 ---
4. inherent internal communication sensitivity around the choices made as part of 

--- Document Chunk 6005 ---
the action plan (non-replacement, redeployment etc.). in addition, given this internal 

--- Document Chunk 6006 ---
redeployment, the pressure on legally binding administrative tasks will increase 

--- Document Chunk 6007 ---
exponentially. 

--- Document Chunk 6008 ---
4

--- Document Chunk 6009 ---
The Agency will indeed tackle this aspect with attention, by highlighting and 

--- Document Chunk 6010 ---
supporting the opportunity of ensuring career paths from administrative tasks to 

--- Document Chunk 6011 ---
operational tasks. natural end-of-contract gate reviews will be used.
